 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>FOR RELEASE AUGUST 11, 2009 5:00 pm Eastern Time </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3SBIO INC. ANNOUNCES UNAUDITED SECOND QUARTER 2009 RESULTS
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Second quarter revenue grew 36.8% year-over-year to RMB81.5 million </I></B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>(US$11.9million); Operating income grew 69.9% year-over-year to RMB25.8 </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>million (US$3.8 million); Company reiterates FY2009 revenue guidance </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>SHENYANG,
CHINA</B> &#151; August&nbsp;11, 2009 &#151; 3SBio Inc. (NASDAQ: SSRX) (&#147;3SBio&#148; or &#147;the Company&#148;), a leading China-based biotechnology company focused on researching, developing, manufacturing and marketing biopharmaceutical
products, today announced its unaudited financial results for the second quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2009. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Second Quarter 2009 Financial Highlights:
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Total net revenues increased by 36.8% over the second quarter of 2008 to RMB81.5 million (US$11.9 million). </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating income increased by 69.9% over the second quarter of 2008 to RMB25.8 million (US$3.8 million) on a GAAP basis, and&nbsp;increased by 60.1% over the second
quarter of 2008 to RMB27.1 million (US$4.0 million) on a non-GAAP basis. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income increased by 39.2% over the second quarter of 2008 to RMB27.0 million (US$4.0 million) on a GAAP basis, and increased by 26.3% over the second quarter of
2008 to RMB26.7 million (US$3.9 million) on a non-GAAP basis. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">3SBio continued to work closely with the State Food and Drug Administration (&#147;SFDA&#148;) to advance the regulatory approval of the three new product programs
submitted in 2008: 36,000 IU dosage formulation of EPIAO, NuLeusin, and TPIAO label extension for the treatment of ITP. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Construction continued on schedule for the Company&#146;s new EPIAO plant, which will support the future growth of EPIAO and serve as the first step towards
exploring global biosimilar opportunities. In June, Mr Deyu Kong joined 3SBio as Director &#150; Manufacture and Process, and will be based in Shenyang. Mr Kong brings a wealth of manufacturing experience under US and EU compliant manufacturing
environments. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">While exports account for a small portion of revenue and the company remains focused on its core business in China, 3SBio and its products EPIAO and TPIAO continue
to be recognized by more physicians and patients in overseas markets. First half export sales grew 45.7% year-over-year and have already exceeded overseas sales for all of 2008. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Dr.&nbsp;Jing Lou, chief executive officer of 3SBio, commented: &#147;We had a good quarter with an encouraging trend in our operating performance. Sales of our leading
products, EPIAO and TPIAO both grew by over 37% due to the strong growth of the dialysis market and our continued efforts to raise awareness of 3SBio in the oncology segment of the market. Our share of the Chinese EPO market now exceeds that of our
five closest competitors combined and we reiterate our 2009 revenue guidance. I am pleased to have Mr.&nbsp;Deyu Kong join us as Director &#150; Manufacture and Process. He will be based in Shenyang where we are expanding our manufacturing capacity
at least four-fold. Mr Kong&#146;s experience with international biotech manufacturing protocols will help us as we explore biosimilar opportunities in the EU and US.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009 Unaudited Financial Results </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Net revenues.</I></B>&nbsp;Net revenues
increased by 36.8% to RMB81.5 million (US$11.9 million) for the second quarter of 2009 from RMB59.6 million (US$8.7 million) for the same period in 2008. This increase was largely due to continued strength from EPIAO and TPIAO products which
increased by 37.6% and 38.4%, respectively, over the same period in 2008. The growth in sales from EPIAO was driven in part by an expanded oncology sales force, which continued to perform well<I>. </I>TPIAO remained 3SBio&#146;s second largest
revenue contributor in the quarter, accounting for 27.3% of total net revenues. Export sales grew by 25.5% to RMB3.5 million (US$0.5 million), and sales of 3SBio&#146;s IV Iron Sucrose rose 42.7% to RMB3.0 million (US$0.4 million). </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Gross profit</I></B><I>. </I>As a result of continued sales growth from key products, gross profit increased by 38.1% to RMB75.0 million (US$11.0 million) for the
second quarter of 2009 from RMB54.3 million (US$7.9 million) for the same period in 2008. Gross margin increased by 0.9% to 92.0% for the second quarter of 2009 from 91.1% for the same period in 2008. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Operating expenses.</I></B><I> </I>GAAP operating expenses were RMB49.2 million (US$7.2 million) for the second quarter of 2009, an increase of 25.8% from GAAP
operating expenses of RMB39.1 million (US$5.7 million) for the same period in 2008. Non-GAAP operating expenses were RMB48.0 million (US$7.0 million) for the second quarter of 2009, an increase of 28.2% from non-GAAP operating expenses of RMB37.4
million (US$ 5.5 million) for the same period in 2008. The increase in operating expenses was largely driven by higher sales&nbsp;and marketing expenses. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

revenue, compared to RMB3.0 million (US$0.4 million), or 5.1% of net revenue for the same period in 2008. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>General and administrative expenses. GAAP </I>general and administrative expenses for the second quarter of 2009 were RMB8.7 million (US$1.3 million),
representing a decrease of 8.7% from general and administrative expenses of RMB9.5million (US$1.4 million) for the same period in 2008. This marked a decline to 10.6% of net revenue for the second quarter of 2009, compared to 15.9% of net revenue
for the second quarter of 2008. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Operating income</I></B><I>. </I>GAAP operating income was RMB25.8 million (US$3.8 million) for
the second quarter of 2009, an increase of 69.<I>9</I>% from operating income of RMB15.2 million (US$2.2 million) for the same period in 2008. Non-GAAP operating income for the second quarter of 2009 grew by 60.1% to RMB27.1 million (US$4.0
million), compared to RMB 17.0&nbsp;million (US$2.5 million) in the second quarter of 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Interest income.</I></B> The Company recorded net
interest income of RMB2.5 million (US$0.4 million) for the second quarter of 2009, compared to RMB5.2 million (US$0.8 million) for the same period in 2008. As experienced in the first quarter of 2009, the decrease in interest income was partially
due to the decrease in the prevailing market interest rates in the second quarter of 2009, compared to the same period in 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Net income.
</I></B>GAAP net income was RMB27.0 million (US$4.0 million) for the second quarter of 2009, 39.2% higher than net income of RMB19.4 million (US$2.8 million) for the same period in 2008. Non-GAAP net income for the second quarter of 2009 was RMB26.7
million (US$3.9 million), 26.3% higher than non-GAAP net income of RMB21.1 million (US$3.1 million) for the second quarter of 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Six months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2009 Unaudited Financial Results </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Net revenues</I></B>. Our net revenues increased by RMB35.1 million, or 30.5%, from RMB115.0
million (US$16.8 million) for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2008 to RMB150.1 million (US$22.0 million) for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009. The increase was primarily attributable to increased sales from our EPIAO and TPIAO products,
underpinned by continued strong demand in the oncology and nephrology markets. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net revenues from EPIAO increased by RMB21.4 million, or 29.5%, to RMB94.0
million (US$13.8 million) for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009. Net revenues from TPIAO increased by RMB9.5 million, or 30.0%, to RMB40.9 million (US$6.0 million) for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009. In addition, revenue from our
export business was RMB6.9 million (US$1.0 million), representing an increase of 45.7% over the first half of 2008, while revenue from our in-licensed Iron Sucrose supplement was RMB5.0 million (US$0.7 million), representing an increase of 44.6%
over the first half of 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Operating income.</I></B> For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009, GAAP operating income increased by 56.3% to
RMB45.9 million (US$6.7 million), compared to RMB29.4 million (US$4.3 million) for the same period in 2008. year. Non-GAAP operating income increased by 51.1% to RMB47.7 million (US$7.0 million), compared to RMB31.6 million (US$4.6 million) for the
same period in 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">GAAP operating margin for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009 was 30.6% as compared to 25.5% for the six months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2008. Non-GAAP operating margin was 31.8% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009, as compared to 27.4% in the same period in 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B><I>Net income.</I></B><I> </I>GAAP net income for the first half of 2009 increased by RMB3.7 million, or 9.5%, to RMB42.9 million (US$6.3million) compared with RMB39.1 million (US$5.7 million) for the same period in 2008. GAAP net margin
for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009 was 28.6% as compared to 34.0% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2008. GAAP net income per ADS for the first half of 2009 increased to RMB1.99 (US$0.29) from RMB1.80 (US$0.26) for the corresponding
period in 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Non-GAAP net income for the first half of 2009 increased by RMB6.3 million, or 15.3%, to RMB47.7 million (US$7.0 million) compared with
RMB41.3 million (US$6.0 million) for the same period in 2008. Non-GAAP net margin for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009 was 31.8% as compared to 35.9% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2008. Non-GAAP net income per ADS for the first half
of 2009 increased to RMB2.21 (US$0.32) from RMB1.90 (US$0.28) for the corresponding period in 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Cash and cash equivalents / Time
deposits.</I></B> 3SBio had positive operating cash flows of RMB 33.2&nbsp;million (US$4.9 million) for the first half of 2009, and as of June&nbsp;30, 2009 retained a strong balance sheet with cash, cash equivalents and time deposits of RMB756.1
million (US$110.7 million), a 3.1% increase from RMB733.0 million (US$107.4 million) as of December&nbsp;31, 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>2009 Full Year Guidance

prepared under any comprehensive set of accounting rules or principals, is not intended to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for the financial information prepared and presented in accordance with GAAP. Non-GAAP measures have limitations
in that they do not reflect all of the amounts associated with the Company&#146;s results of operations as determined in accordance with GAAP. These measures should only be used to evaluate the Company&#146;s results of operations in conjunction
with the corresponding GAAP measures. Please see the attached reconciliation of GAAP to non-GAAP for an explanation of the amounts excluded to arrive at non-GAAP financial measures for the three-month periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2008 and
June&nbsp;30, 2009 and for the six month periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2009 and June&nbsp;30, 2008. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Statement Regarding Unaudited Financial Information

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>About 3SBio Inc. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"

pharmaceutical products in China; market acceptance of 3SBio products; expected hospital or patient demand for our products; the completion of 3SBio&#146;s ongoing clinical trials as planned; receipt and timing of regulatory approvals for
3SBio&#146;s new products and uses; 3SBio&#146;s ability to expand its production, sales and distribution network and other aspects of its operations; its ability to effectively protect its intellectual property; changes in the healthcare industry
